The variety of the buffet is much less, but there are few people, there is no way, the quantity is small, but the portion is not large, except for the barbecue early closing stall, the food is still sufficient until I leave. I can understand that it is not easy to operate the hotel during this time. The one I want to complain about is the sushi chef. The sea bream was fine, the tuna was rotten bit by bit, and it was not piece by piece. It was very strange, but there were few people on that day, so the portions were quite large. foot. Also the rest of the hotel staff was not polite on first visit. There is a pack of Lipton green tea in my room that has been placed for a long time, and the back is rotten. I can see that the date is 2021, but everything else is fine. There is nothing to complain about the hotel. If you come here now, the overall cost performance is not as high as before.
